These  Schools  prepare  pupils  thoroughly  for  commercial  pursuits 
ill  all  lines;  also  for  practical  work  in  all  the  Engineering  profes- 
sions. The  success  of  their  graduates  is  well  known  to  the  whole 
commimity. 

HEALD'S    COLLEGE 

Has  become  a  household  word  all  over  the  Pacific  Coast,  as  it  has 
stood  in  the  front  i-ank  of  our  Educational  institutions  for  forty-three 
years. 

PUPILS    CAN   ATTEND    EITHER    SCHOOL. 

Pupils  paying  at  one  school  can  attend  the  other  school  if  found 
more  convenient.  Both  schools  are  thoroughly  up  to  date  in  their 
methods. 

POSITIONS    rOR    GRADUATES. 

The  Heald  Colleges  have  always  made  it  a  point  to  take  care  of 
its  pupils  and  to  furnish  situations  to  all  worthy  graduates.  No 
pains  will  be  spared  in  the  future  to  find  employment  for  those  who 
attend  any  of  its  Associated  Colleges. 

HEALD'S  SCHOOL   OF  ENGINEERING 

Gives  pupils  a  scientific  and  practical  training  in  Mining  Engineering, 
Electrical  Engineering,  Civil  Engineering,  Steam  Engineering  and 
Gas  Engineering. 

RATES   OF   TUITION 

Are  as  low  as  is  consistent  with  first  class  instruction.  The  HEALD 
Schools  stand  for  quality,  and  any  one  patronizing  them  knows  he 
will  get  the  best  that  is  to  be  had  in  the  Educational  line.  This  is 
why  their  graduates  are  invariably  successful  in  their  callings. 

FULL  INFORMATION

ments by  addressing 

E.  P.  HEALI>,  President 

1451   Franklin  Street
